Internally, the skin may feel like it has red and black spots resembling peach or plum rashes, accompanied by numbness in the hands and feet, where pinpricks do not cause pain. The soles of the feet may hurt so much that one struggles to stand. During meals, when opening the mouth to breathe, there may be strange sounds, and speech can be similar. The body might develop sores and itchiness that feel like crawling insects, or the elbows may feel constricted. This condition is called Black Leprosy, also known as Black Spot.

For those suffering from White Leprosy, their voice is hoarse, vision is unclear, limbs are sore and painful, the body is very hot, and there is an inner feeling of irritation. The hands and feet move slowly, and there is tension in the back. It may feel like being pricked by needles inside, and sometimes rashes may develop. Often, the white spots are located within the skin, there can be polyps in the nose, or white pearls may appear in the eyes, obstructing vision. This condition is referred to as White Leprosy.[47p]

　　　　　(疒咅)(疒畾)

　　夫人阳气外虚则多汗，汗出当风，风气搏于肌肉，与热气并则生(疒咅)(疒畾)，状如麻豆，甚者渐大，搔之则成疮也。
　　　　　紫癜风

　　夫紫癜风者，由皮肤生紫点，搔之皮起，而不痒痛者是也。此皆风湿邪气客于腠理，与气血相搏，致荣卫否濇，风冷在于肌肉之间，故令色紫也。
　　　　　白癜风

　　夫肺有壅热，又风气外伤于肌肉，热与风交并，邪毒之气，伏留于腠理，与卫气相搏，不能消散，令皮肤皴起生白斑，故名白瘢风也。
　　　　　白驳

　　《病源论》云：风白驳者，面及颈项身体皮肉色变白，与肉色不同，亦不痒痛，谓之白驳。此亦是风邪搏于皮肤，血气不和所生也。　　夫白驳者，是肺风流注皮肤之间，久而不去之所致也。多生于项面，点点斑白，但无疮，及不发痒，不能早疗，即便浸淫也。[48p]

The following text discusses various skin conditions related to wind and dampness in Traditional Chinese Medicine:

  1. (Nèihǔ) and (Nèiyuán): When the body's Yang energy is weak externally, excessive sweating occurs, especially when exposed to wind. This wind interacts with the muscles and, combined with heat, produces (Nèihǔ)(Nèiyuán), resembling small beans. In severe cases, these can grow larger and scratching them can lead to sores.

  2. Purple Spot Disease: This condition is characterized by the emergence of purple spots on the skin. Scratching causes the skin to rise without itch or pain. It is believed to result from wind and damp evil qi affecting the pores, clashing with the body's qi and blood, disrupting the balance of protective and nourishing forces, and causing the skin to take on a purple hue due to cold wind trapped between the muscles.

  3. White Spot Disease: This arises when there is obstruction of heat in the lungs, and wind externally injures the muscles. The interaction between heat and wind leads to the accumulation of harmful toxins in the pores, which struggles against the protective qi and cannot disperse. This creates raised, white patches on the skin, resulting in what is called white spot disease.

  4. White Fleck: According to "Bingyuan Lun", white flecks appear on the face, neck, and skin, differing in color from normal flesh and are not itchy or painful, hence referred to as white fleck. This condition stems from wind evil affecting the skin and a disharmony in blood energies. White fleck results from wind in the lungs invading the skin, and if it persists without treatment, it can lead to long-lasting conditions. These tend to appear around the neck and face as small white spots without sores and lacking itch, making early treatment difficult, even when immersed in the condition.[48p]

　　　　　疬疡风

　　夫风邪积热，居于肺腑，久而不散，流溢皮肤，令人颈边胸前腋下，自然斑驳点点相连，其色微白而圆，亦有紫色者，亦无痛痒，谓之疬疡风也。凡此皆风热伏留肌腠之间，气血不和，乃生此疾也。
　　　　医门法律 【清　喻昌】

　　　　　论疠风

　　凡治疠风之法，以清荣卫为主，其汗宜频发，血宜频刺，皆清荣卫之捷法也。生虫由于肺热，其清肃之令不行，故由皮毛渐及腠理，肠胃莫不有虫，清其金则虫不驱自熄。试观金风一动，旱魃绝踪，其理明矣。然清肺亦必先清荣卫，盖荣卫之气，腐而不清，传入于肺，先害其清肃之令故也。苦药虽能泻肝杀虫，亦能伤胃，不可久服。胃者，荣卫从出之源也，久服苦寒，荣卫转衰，而腐败壅郁，不可胜言矣。所以苦参丸之类，荣卫素弱谷食不充之人，不宜服也。大枫子油，最能杀虫驱风，然复过于辛热，风未除而目先坏者多矣。[49p]

Wind Pestilence

Wind pathogen accumulates heat and dwells in the lungs. If it remains for a long time without dispersing, it overflows into the skin, causing spots and patches to naturally connect around the neck, chest, and armpits. These spots are slightly white and round, with some appearing purplish; they are neither painful nor itchy, referred to as wind pestilence. All of this is due to wind heat remaining lodged between the skin layers, causing disharmony in qi and blood, thus giving rise to this illness.

Discussion on Pestilential Wind

In treating pestilential wind, the primary focus is on cleansing the defensive and nutritive qi. Sweating should be encouraged frequently, and bloodletting should be done often, as these are quick methods to clear the defensive and nutritive qi. The presence of parasites is due to heat in the lungs, which prevents the qi from effectively dispersing. Thus, it gradually affects the skin and muscle layers, and there are parasites in the intestines and stomach. By cleansing the metal (lungs), the parasites will self-extinguish. When wind gold stirs, drought demons disappear, illustrating this principle clearly. However, to clear the lungs, one must first cleanse the defensive and nutritive qi, as their corruption prevents proper function and impairs the lung's purifying command. Bitter medicinals can purge the liver and kill parasites, but they can also harm the stomach and should not be taken for long periods. The stomach is the source of the emergence of defensive and nutritive qi. Prolonged use of bitter cold treatments causes the nutritive and defensive qi to weaken, leading to corruption and stagnation, which is difficult to express completely. Therefore, formulas like Ku Shen Wan should not be taken by those with weak defensive and nutritive qi who do not consume enough food. Semen Euphorbiae is particularly effective for killing parasites and expelling wind, yet it is overly hot and pungent, often causing damage to the eyes before the wind is expelled.[49p]

其硫黄酒服之，必致脑裂之祸。又醉仙散入轻粉和末，日进三服，取其人昏昏若醉，毒涎从齿缝中出，疠未瘥而齿先落矣。盖除疠之药，服之近而少，疠必不除；服之久且多，疠虽除，药之贻害更大。惟易老驱风丸、东坡四神丹二方，可以久服取效，取为法焉。　　要知脉风成则为疠，然人之荣血，正行于十二经脉之中者也，用平善之药，生血清热为主，驱风杀虫为辅，更行汗之刺之之法，无不愈者。且非极意惩创之人不可与治，以戒色欲禁口腹二者，非烈汉不能也。耆婆《恶病论》曰：疾风有四百四种，总而言之，不出五种，即是五风所摄云。[50p]

If one consumes sulfuric wine, it will surely lead to the calamity of split brains. Moreover, taking drunken immortal powder mixed with light powder thrice daily will leave the person in a daze as if drunk, with toxic saliva oozing between the teeth, and while the plague may not be cured, the teeth will fall out first. Indeed, for the medicine to eliminate the plague, taking it infrequently and in small amounts will ensure it is ineffective; yet taking it for a long time and in large amounts may eliminate the plague, but the harm from the medicine will be even greater. Only the Easy Aging Wind-Dispelling Pill and Dongpo's Four Divine Pills can be taken for a long time to achieve results and be considered the proper method.

It is essential to know that when the pulse wind manifests, it becomes a plague. However, the essential blood of a person flows through the twelve channels. Using balanced and good medicines, focusing on generating blood and clearing heat as the main approach, and using wind-dispelling and insect-killing as supplements, along with practices that induce sweat and needling, will heal all. Furthermore, it is necessary that those who are extremely intent on punishing their own wounds cannot be treated, implying abstention from sensual desires and controlling hunger; only strong men can do this. Qibo's "On Evil Diseases" states: "The swift wind has four hundred and four types, but in summary, it does not exceed five types; these are the five winds that govern all."[50p]

何名五风？一曰黄风，二曰青风，三曰白风，四曰赤风，五曰黑风。其风合五脏，故曰五风。五风生五虫，黄风生黄虫，青风生青虫，白风生白虫，赤风生赤虫，黑风生黑虫。此五种虫食人五脏，若食人脾，语变声散；若食人肝，眉睫堕落；若食人心，遍身生疮，若食人肺，鼻柱崩倒，鼻中生息肉，若食人肾，耳鸣啾啾，或如车行雷鼓之声；若食人皮，皮肤顽痹；若食人筋，肢节堕落。五风合五脏，虫生至多入于骨髓，来去无碍，坏于人身，名曰疾风。疾风者，是疠病之根本也。病之初起，或如针锥所刺，名曰刺风；或如虫走，名曰游风；遍身掣动，名曰瞤风；不觉痛痒，名曰顽风。[51p]

What are the five winds? The first is the Yellow Wind, the second the Green Wind, the third the White Wind, the fourth the Red Wind, and the fifth the Black Wind. These winds correspond to the five viscera, hence they are called the Five Winds. The Five Winds produce the Five Worms: the Yellow Wind produces the Yellow Worm, the Green Wind produces the Green Worm, the White Wind produces the White Worm, the Red Wind produces the Red Worm, and the Black Wind produces the Black Worm. These five types of worms feast upon the five viscera of humans. If they consume the spleen, the speech becomes confused; if they consume the liver, the eyebrows and lashes fall; if they consume the heart, sores appear all over the body; if they consume the lungs, the nasal bridge collapses, and polyps grow within the nose; if they consume the kidneys, there is ringing in the ears, either like the sound of a car or thunder; if they consume the skin, it becomes hard and stiff; if they consume the tendons, the limbs become weak and fall apart. The Five Winds correspond to the Five Viscera, and the worms infiltrate the bones and marrow the most, coming and going without obstruction, damaging the human body, and are called the Swift Wind. The Swift Wind is the root of plague. When illness first arises, it may feel like being pricked by needles, known as the Stabbing Wind; or it may feel like crawling insects, known as the Creeping Wind; or it may cause painful contractions throughout the body, known as the Twitching Wind; or it may cause unnoticed pain and itching, known as the Stubborn Wind.[51p]

肉起如桃李小枣核，从头而起者，名曰顺风；从两脚起者，名曰逆风。如连钱团圆，赤白青乌斑驳，名曰疠风。或遍体生疮，或如疥癣，或如鱼鳞，或如榆荚，或如钱孔，或痛或痒，黄汁流出，肢节坏烂，悉为脓血，或不痒不痛，或起或灭，青黄赤白黑，变易不定。病起之由，皆因冷热交通，流入五脏，通彻骨髓，用力过度，饮食相违，房室不节，虚劳动极，汗流遍体；因兹积热彻五脏，饮食杂秽，虫生至多，食人五脏骨髓皮肉筋节，久久败坏，名曰疠风。是故论曰：若欲疗之，先服阿魏雷丸散出虫，看其形状青黄赤白黑，然后与药疗，千万无有不差。人得此疾，速宜弃家室财物，入山静养疗治，无有不差。[52p]

When flesh rises like the small pits of peaches and jujubes, if it arises from the head, it is called "favorable wind"; if it arises from the feet, it is called "adverse wind." If there are patches resembling scattered coins, mottled red, white, blue, and black, it is called "pestilential wind." Some may have sores all over the body, or resemble scabies, or fish scales, or elm pods, or coin holes, experiencing either pain or itchiness, with yellow fluid flowing out, and limbs rotting, all full of pus and blood. Some may be neither itchy nor painful, may arise or disappear, in shades of blue, yellow, red, white, or black, changing unpredictably. The cause of this illness is due to the interplay of hot and cold affecting the five organs, penetrating to the marrow, resulting from excessive exertion, conflicting diet, unregulated sexual activity, or excessive labor causing sweating all over the body. Consequently, accumulated heat penetrates the five organs, with impure diet leading to an abundance of worms that consume the five organs, marrow, skin, flesh, and tendons, resulting in decay over time, called "pestilential wind." Therefore, it is said: if one wishes to treat this, one should first take a pill made from ferula (asafoetida) to expel the worms, observe their shape, whether blue, yellow, red, white, or black, and then administer medication, ensuring precision. If one contracts this illness, it is advisable to quickly abandon home, family, and possessions, retreat to the mountains for quiet recuperation, and treatment, ensuring no mistakes are made.[52p]

　　　　景岳全书 【明　张介宾】

　　　　　论证

　　疠风，即大风也，又谓之癞风，俗又名为大麻风。此病虽名为风，而实非外感之风也。实以天地间阴厉浊恶之邪，或受风木之化而风热化虫，或受湿毒于皮毛而后及营卫，或犯不洁，或因传染，皆得生虫。盖虫者厥阴主之，厥阴为风木，主生五虫也。虫之生也，初不为意，而渐久渐多，遂致不可解救，诚最恶最危最丑证也。又《千金》云：自作不仁，极恶之业也，所以最为难治。观孙真人云：尝治数百人，终无一人免于死者，盖无一人能守禁忌故耳。[53p]

Discussion of Evidence

Pestilential wind, also known as great wind, is also called leprosy wind and commonly referred to as great leprosy. Although this disease is named "wind," it is not caused by the external influence of wind. Instead, it arises from the malevolent evils present in the yin and filthy air of heaven and earth, where it may either transform due to the influence of wind and wood, causing heat and the emergence of insects, or it may arise from damp toxins in the skin and fur, subsequently affecting the body's defensive and nutritive qi. It can also result from uncleanliness or from contagion, all of which lead to the birth of insects. In essence, these insects are governed by the Liver's yin, which is associated with wind and wood, and is responsible for the emergence of various insects. The initial occurrence of the insects is not intentional, but as time goes on, they multiply, leading to a situation that is irredeemable. This is indeed the most malign, perilous, and disgraceful manifestation. Moreover, the "Thousand Gold" text states: "Those who act unkindly are engaged in the most heinous acts, making it extremely difficult to treat." Observing the words of Master Sun, he mentioned that he treated hundreds of patients, yet not a single one escaped death, for none adhered to the necessary prohibitions.[53p]

惟一妇人病愈，后又服加减四物汤百余剂，半年之上，方得经行，十分全愈。又丹溪治五人，亦惟一妇人得免，以其贫甚且寡，无物可吃也；外三四人者，越二三年皆复作而死。由此观之，可见此证非得出奇秘方，鲜能取效。故余逢此证，不敢强以为知而妄施治疗，亦不敢强言治法以惑后人。至若古人论治之法，亦甚详悉，用之得宜，虽病根未必可拔，而延保余年，夭枉亦自可免。由是遍求诸说，则惟薛立斋《疠疡机要》论列已全。　　疠疡之有兼证变证，凡如表里脏腑诸病，无不有之，其各治法巳悉各门，但有所值，即宜随证参用之，左右逢源，无弗善也。重录资繁，兹不赘及。
　　　　　禁忌

　　患斯疾者，多由嗜欲不谨所致。治斯疾者，速当断戒荤腥盐酱一切厚味，只宜清心寡欲，绝色忘虑，幽隐林泉，屏弃世务，早早救疗，庶几可活。稍不守禁，每愈而复作，及致危剧，莫能再救，总以不守禁忌也。[54p]

Only one woman recovered from illness; after taking a modified Si Wu Decoction for over a hundred doses, she finally regained her menstruation after more than half a year, achieving complete recovery. Among the five patients treated by Danxi, only one woman escaped death due to her extreme poverty and lack of food; the other three or four individuals relapsed and died after two or three years. From this, it can be seen that extraordinary secret prescriptions are rarely effective in such cases. Therefore, when I encounter such conditions, I do not dare to hastily claim knowledge and recklessly apply treatments, nor do I boldly assert treatment methods that may mislead future generations. As for the ancient methods discussed in treatments, they are indeed very thorough; when applied appropriately, even if the root cause of the disease may not be completely eradicated, one can still prolong their years and avoid premature death. Thus, after extensive inquiry into various opinions, Xue Lijia's "Essentials of Epidemic Diseases" stands out as the most comprehensive.

Epidemic diseases often feature accompanying or changing symptoms; all types of illnesses caused by internal or external organs have these characteristics, and their respective treatment methods have already been articulated in various schools. One should appropriately adapt treatments based on the symptoms presented, ensuring comprehensive support, as all methods can yield good outcomes. Due to the extensive information available, I shall not elaborate further on this matter.

Prohibitions

Those suffering from this illness often do so due to a lack of restraint in their desires. To treat this illness, one must promptly cease consuming meat, strong flavors, salty sauces, and all heavy foods, and instead cultivate a calm heart and minimal desires, avoiding distractions and immersing oneself in natural surroundings. One should also abandon worldly concerns and seek treatment early; doing so may increase the chance of survival. If one does not adhere to these prohibitions, relapses are likely, leading to severe consequences that may be beyond remedy; this is all due to the failure to observe these restrictions.[54p]

　　　　石室秘箓 【清　陈士铎】

　　　　　治法

　　瘴疠者，乃两粤之气，郁蒸而变之者也。其气皆热而非寒，其证皆头痛而腹满。土人服槟榔无碍者，辛以散之也。盖火气得寒，反抑郁而不伸，槟榔气辛，同气易入，其味却散，故适与病相宜。然止可救一时之急，终不可恃之为长城也。今立一方，可长治瘴疠之侵。人参、半夏、槟榔各一钱，白朮五钱，茯苓、麦冬各三钱，陈皮、甘草、枳壳、柴胡各五分，五味子五粒，水煎服。比方之妙，全非治瘴疠之品，而服之自消。盖健脾则气旺，气旺则瘴疠不能相侵，即既感者，方中亦有去瘴疠之药，岂有不奏功立应者乎？此瘴疠治法，又宜知之也。　　或人有感疠而成大麻风者，又不可如是治法。[55p]

Secret Prescription for the Stone Chamber
By Chen Shiduo of the Qing Dynasty

Method of Treatment

Epidemic diseases are related to the miasma of the Two Guangdong regions, transformed by heat and humidity. The qi is predominantly hot rather than cold, and the symptoms include headaches and abdominal fullness. Locals who consume areca nut are not harmed by it as it disperses the symptoms due to its pungency. The essence of fire, when cooled by cold, becomes suppressed and unable to manifest; thus, the pungent nature of areca nut readily enters the body and its flavor effectively disperses, making it appropriate for the illness. However, it can only alleviate urgent situations temporarily and should not be relied upon as a permanent solution.

Now, I establish a formula to continuously combat the invasion of miasma. Use one qian each of ginseng, pinellia, and areca nut; five qians of white atractylodes; three qians each of poria and ophiopogon; five fen each of tangerine peel, licorice, bitter orange peel, and bupleurum; and five grains of schisandra. Boil these in water and take them.

The wonders of this formula do not originate from what is typically used to treat miasma, but rather, it alleviates the condition itself. Strengthening the spleen enhances qi, which in turn prevents miasma from invading. For those already affected, the formula contains herbs that expel miasma—how could it fail to yield effective results? This method of treating miasma is important to understand. However, if someone suffers from miasma and develops severe leprosy, this treatment is not appropriate.[55p]

盖大麻风纯是热毒之气，裹于皮肤之间，湿气又藏遏于肌骨之内，所以外证皮红生点，须眉尽落，遍体腐烂，臭气既不可闻，人又安肯近而与治？余心痛之，乃立一奇方，用元参、苍朮、熟地、苍耳子、薏仁、茯苓各四两，名为四六汤，各为末，蜜为丸，每日吞用一两，二料必然全愈。盖此方之妙，能补肾健脾，而加入散风去湿，正补则邪自退，不必治大风而大风自治矣。急宜先刻一张，广行施舍，功德又何可量哉？止忌房事而已。又方用槟榔一钱，柴胡八分，白朮、白芍、白芥子、茯苓各三钱，车前子二钱，枳壳五分，水煎服。有火加黄连五分，水煎服。二剂即瘴消，亦妙方也。　　大麻风，余有奇方，用苍朮、熟地、元参、苍耳子、白芥子、车前子、生甘草各二两，金银花十两，蒲公英四两，各为末，蜜丸，一料全愈。[56p]

Leprosy is primarily caused by the accumulation of pathogenic heat and toxins, which envelop the skin, while dampness is concealed within the muscles and bones. This results in external symptoms such as redness of the skin, loss of hair, and widespread rotting, emitting a stench that makes it unbearable for anyone to approach for treatment. I feel a deep sorrow for this, so I devised a unique formula using four taels each of Yuan Shen, Cang Zhu, Shu Di, Cang Er Zi, Yi Ren, and Fu Ling, named the Six-Four Decoction. Each ingredient is ground into a powder and made into pills with honey. Taking one tael daily will surely lead to complete recovery. The brilliance of this formula lies in its ability to tonify the kidney and strengthen the spleen, while also dispersing wind and eliminating dampness. When the body is properly nourished, the pathogens naturally retreat, so there is no need to directly treat the leprosy itself—it will resolve on its own. It’s recommended to have this printed and distributed widely; the merits of this act cannot be quantified. One should only avoid sexual activity.

Additionally, there is another formula using one qian of betel nut, eight fen of Chai Hu, and three qian each of Bai Zhu, Bai Shao, Bai Jiao Zi, and Fu Ling, with two qian of Che Qian Zi and five fen of Zhi Ke, all boiled in water for oral consumption. If there is heat, add five fen of Huang Lian and boil again for oral consumption. Two doses will alleviate the condition as well, which is also a remarkable formula.

For leprosy, I have yet another extraordinary formula using two taels each of Cang Zhu, Shu Di, Yuan Shen, Cang Er Zi, Bai Jiao Zi, Che Qian Zi, and fresh Gan Cao, along with ten taels of Jin Yin Hua and four taels of Pu Gong Ying, all ground into a powder and made into pills. One dose will lead to complete recovery.[56p]

　　　　方

　　桦皮散 【河间，下同。】治肺痈风毒，遍身瘾疹搔痒。　　枳壳　桦皮各四两，并炒存性　甘草炙，半两　杏仁去皮尖，水一碗，煎令减半，取出，令干，另研　荆芥穗各二两　　右为末，每服二钱，食后温酒调下。[57p]

Recipe for Birch Bark Powder

This formula treats lung abscesses caused by wind and toxins, as well as skin rashes and itching all over the body.

Ingredients:

  • Bitter Orange Peel: 4 ounces (stir-fried until ready)
  • Birch Bark: 4 ounces (stir-fried until ready)
  • Licorice Root (prepared): 0.5 ounces
  • Almonds (peeled and pointed ends removed): 0.5 ounces
  • Water: 1 bowl (reduce to half through boiling)

Preparation:
After taking the reduced liquid, let it dry and grind it separately. Add:

  • Japanese Catnip: 2 ounces

Combine everything into a fine powder. The dosage is 2 qian (a traditional unit of weight) per serving, taken with warm wine after meals.[57p]

　　二圣散　疏风和血。
　　大黄半两　皂角刺三钱
　　右将皂角刺烧灰研细，用大黄半两，煎汤调下二钱。早服桦皮散，以升麻汤下泻青丸；晚服二圣散，此为缓治。
　　补气泻荣汤 【东垣】
　　升麻　连翘各六分　苏木　当归　全蝎　黄连　地龙去土　黄芪各五分　黄芩生，四分　桔梗五分　人参二分　生地四分　桃仁三粒　甘草一分半　梧桐泪一分　水蛭三条，炒烟尽　蝱虫去翅足微炒，三个　麝香少许　　右剉如麻豆大。除连翘另銼；梧桐泪研白豆蔻二分为细末，二味另放；麝香、蝱虫、水蛭三味为末，另放外，都作一服，水二大盏，酒一匙，入连翘煎至一盏六分；再入梧桐泪、白豆蔻二味，并麝香等三味，再上火煎一二沸，去渣稍热，早饭后午饭前服。忌酒湿面生冷鞕物。[58p]

Er Sheng San: Disperse wind and harmonize blood.
Ingredients: Half a tael of rhubarb, three qian of prickly ash.
Prepare by burning and grinding the prickly ash to a fine powder. Mix half a tael of rhubarb, decoct it, and add two qian of the powder. Take the birch bark powder with the Angelica decoction to aid in expelling the Blue Pill in the morning; take Er Sheng San in the evening as a gentle treatment.

Bu Qi Xie Rong Tang 【Dong Yuan】:
Six fen each of Angelica, Forsythia; five fen each of Senegalia, Dong Quai, whole scorpion, Coptis, and Earthworm without soil; four fen of fresh Radix Scutellaria; five fen of Platycodon; two fen of Ginseng; four fen of fresh Rehmannia; three peach kernels; one and a half fen of licorice; one fen of Wutong sap; three fried leeches until smoke dissipates; three wingless and lightly roasted grasshoppers; a small amount of musk.
Chop the herbs to the size of a large bean. Grind Forsythia separately; finely powder Wutong sap with two fen of cardamom; keep separate. Powder musk, grasshoppers, and leeches; keep separately as well. Combine all into one dose. Use two big bowls of water and one spoonful of wine, adding the Forsythia to decoct until down to one bowl and six fen. Then add Wutong sap, cardamom, musk, and the three powdered items, bringing to a boil one or two times. Strain, slightly warm, and take before breakfast and before lunch. Avoid wine, damp foods, and cold unripe items.[58p]

　　醉仙散 【《宝鉴》】　 治疠风遍身麻木。　　胡麻子炒　牛蒡子炒　枸杞子　蔓荆子炒，各－两　白蒺藜　苦参　防风　(艹舌)蒌根各五钱　　右为细末，每一两五钱，入轻粉二钱拌匀，每服一钱，茶清调，晨午各一服，至五七日，于牙缝中出臭涎，令人如醉，或下脓血，病根乃去。仍量人病之轻重虚实用，病重者须先以再造散下之，候元气将复，方用此药。忌一切炙煿厚味，止可食淡粥时菜。诸蛇，以淡酒蒸熟食之，可以助药力。

Drunken Immortal Powder (From "Treasure Mirror")

For the treatment of widespread numbness due to pestilential wind:

Ingredients:

  • Fried sesame seeds
  • Fried burdock seeds
  • Goji berries
  • Fried rhamnus fruit, each two taels
  • White spiny thistle
  • Bitter sofnoria
  • Siler root (with a tongue-like shape)
  • Five qian each of the last three ingredients.

Grind these into a fine powder. Take one and a half taels of this powder, mix it with two qian of light powder uniformly. Take one qian each time, dissolved in clear tea, morning and afternoon, for a total of five to seven days, until foul saliva emerges from between the teeth, causing a feeling of intoxication; this may also lead to purulent blood, thus removing the root of the illness. Adjust based on the severity of the individual's condition; those with severe disease must first take "Rebuilding Powder," wait for the vital energy to recover before using this medicine. Avoid all roasted, strong flavors and only eat light porridge with vegetables. For snakes, steam them with light alcohol and consume to enhance the medicinal effects.

Heavenly Rebuilding Powder
For the treatment of severe wind pestilence.

Ingredients:

  • Half a tael of turmeric
  • Cooked rhubarb
  • Fried black soapwort thorns (large ones), each one tael
  • Six qian of white morning glory, half raw and half fried.

Grind these into a powder. Take five qian each time, before sunrise, facing east, mixed with unburnt alcohol for consumption.

　　海藏愈风丹　治疠病手足麻木，眉毛脱落，遍身生疮；及疠风瘾疹，皮肤瘙痒，搔破成疮，并皆主之。　　苦参一斤，取末四两　皂角一斤，銼寸许无灰酒浸一宿，以水一碗，挼成汁去渣入砂器中，文武火熬　土花蛇一条，去肠，阴干酒浸，取净肉晒干为末，大风证用之　白花蛇　乌梢蛇各取一条，依前酒浸，取肉为末　　右为末，入前二味，和丸梧子大，每服六七十丸，空心，煎通圣散送下，干物压之，日三服，间日浴之，汗出为度。　　愚按前方果系疠风，用之必效。若肝经血热，脾经血虚，肾经虚火，脾肺气虚，遍身作痒，搔破成疮，或内热生风，而眉鬓脱落，或皮肤赤晕，或搔起白屑，而类疠风者，服之反成疠风矣。[62p]

Haicang Yufeng Pill: Treats ailments that cause numbness in the hands and feet, loss of eyebrows, and sores all over the body; also used for epidemic wind rashes, skin itchiness, and sores from scratching. Ingredients: one jin of KuShen, ground to four liang; one jin of Soap Pod, finely shredded and soaked in no-ash wine overnight, then mixed with a bowl of water, strained, and placed in a sand pot for slow boiling; one snake (Tuhua She), eviscerated, dried in the shade, soaked in wine, then the clean meat dried and ground into powder; one each of white flower snake and black tipped snake, similarly prepared. Combine the powders of the first two ingredients and form into pills the size of a wutong seed; take sixty to seventy pills on an empty stomach, washed down with Tongsheng Powder, and press down with dry substances. Take three times a day, or every other day, and bathe to induce sweating as needed.

Note: This treatment is specifically for epidemic wind. It must be effective. However, if there is heat in the liver channel, blood deficiency in the spleen channel, empty fire in the kidney channel, or deficient qi in the spleen and lungs leading to generalized itching and sores from scratching, or if internal heat causes wind leading to loss of hair, or if there are red rashes on the skin or white flakes appearing from scratching, then taking this remedy may worsen the condition.[62p]

　　苦参消石酒　浸酒法见后。
　　苦参　消石　清酒
　　右三味，先用清酒下消石浸之二七日或三七日，然后与苦参同入酒瓮中盛浸之七日，渐渐服之。饮法：空腹服之，一日三服。初七日中一服如半鸡子许，七日后可饮一升，任情饮之，多则为善，患去则速。风动亦多，勿使醉吐，宁渐少饮，不用多饮。赤白二风，此药至口，无有不愈，余非难治。何以故？热为根本，故苦参能治热，消石除热消虫，赤白二虫，但闻消石气，皆变为水，能去热根本。[63p]

Kushen Stone-Dissolving Wine; the method of infusion is explained below.

Ingredients: Kushen, Stone-Dissolving, Clear Wine.

Take these three ingredients and first infuse the Stone-Dissolving in Clear Wine for either twenty-seven days or thirty-seven days. Then, combine with Kushen and place into a wine jar to steep for seven days, gradually consuming it.

Dosage: Take on an empty stomach, three times a day. During the first seven days, consume about the size of a half egg at a time. After seven days, you may drink up to a liter, as much as you feel inclined. The more you consume, the better; the illness will diminish quickly. If you experience excessive wind movement, avoid getting drunk or vomiting; it is better to drink less gradually rather than too much all at once.

This remedy is effective against both red and white wind; for this medicine, it is guaranteed to heal all ailments. Other illnesses are not difficult to treat. Why? Because heat is the root cause. Thus, Kushen can treat heat, and the Stone-Dissolving eliminates heat and expels worms. For both red and white worms, merely inhaling the essence of the Stone-Dissolving will turn them into water, effectively addressing the root of heat.[63p]

若患赤白二风，不问年月，多者五年以外，加黄消石、加酒、苦参乃至三四两，无有不愈。乃至三十年，无鼻柱肢节堕落者，但非黑虫，皆得永愈。第一忌房室，大嗔怒，大热食；禁粘食五辛生冷大酢酪白酒，猪鱼鸡犬驴马牛羊等肉，皆为大忌，其余不禁。此为对治，非正治也。若人顽痹不觉痛痒处者，当作大白膏药摩之，一日三四度，七日彻，或二三七日彻，乃至七七四十九日，名曰一大彻。顽痹即觉痒平复如本，即止摩。若不平复，但使摩之，以瘥为限。不过两大彻三大彻，无有不愈。针刺灸烧割劫，亦不及摩之为良。乃至身上多有疮痕生，摩之悉愈。[64p]

If one suffers from the dual afflictions of red and white wind, regardless of how long it has been, even after five years, adding yellow消石, alcohol, and bitter herbs (such as苦参) in quantities of three to four taels will lead to recovery. Even after thirty years, if there is no falling away of the nose, fingers, or joints, and provided there are no black worms, all can achieve lasting recovery. First, avoid sexual activity, excessive anger, and hot foods. Refrain from sticky foods, five pungent vegetables, cold dishes, strong vinegars, alcohol, and meats like pork, fish, chicken, dog, donkey, horse, and lamb; all these are major prohibitions, while other foods are not restricted. This is a treatment method, not a fundamental cure. If someone experiences stubborn numbness without feeling pain or itchiness in certain areas, they should apply a thick white plaster and massage it three to four times a day for seven days, or continue for two or three sessions of seven days each, up to a total of forty-nine days, which is termed one complete treatment. If the numbness resolves and the itchiness subsides as before, one should stop massaging. If it does not resolve, continue to massage until healed. Generally, two or three complete treatments will suffice for recovery. Techniques like acupuncture, moxibustion, or incisions are not as effective as this method of massage. Even if one has many scars, massaging them will surely lead to healing.[64p]

　　大白膏
　　白芷　白朮　前胡　吴茱萸各一升　蜀椒　细辛各三两　当归　桂心各二两　苦酒四升　芎藭二升　　右十味，以苦酒浸药经一宿，取不中水猪脂十斤，铜器中煎令沸，三上三下，候白芷色黄，膏成，贮以瓶中，随病摩之即愈。若遍体生疮，脓血溃坏，当作大黑膏摩之。

Great White Ointment
1 sheng of Bai Zhi, Bai Zhu, Qian Hu, and Wu Zhu Yu; 3 liang of Shu Jiao and Xi Xin; 2 liang of Dang Gui and Gui Xin; 4 sheng of bitter wine; 2 sheng of Xiong Dan.
Mix these ten ingredients and soak them in bitter wine overnight. Then take 10 jin of non-water pig fat, boil in a copper vessel until it bubbles, stirring it three times up and down, and wait until the color of Bai Zhi turns yellow; the ointment is then formed. Store it in a bottle and apply to the affected area for immediate healing. If there are sores all over the body with pus and blood, use the Great Black Ointment instead.

Great Black Ointment
½ liang of Wu Tou, Xiong Dan, Xiong Huang, Hu Fen, Mu Fang Ji, Mu Ma, Huang Lian, Ci Huang, Li Lu, and Fan Shi; 40 pieces each of Ba Dou and peeled Xing Ren; 1.8 qian of Huang Bo; a piece of pine resin and miscellaneous hair each about the size of an egg.
Grind these fifteen ingredients into powder, mix with 2 jin of pig fat, and then boil until the fat is fully dissolved into an ointment. Apply to the sores three times a day, after washing with saline water, and then applying the ointment. Keep away from women, children, and pets. If the affected person's eyebrows and eyelashes have fallen out and do not grow back, after taking the medicine for 100 days, apply iron paste to the areas where the eyebrows and eyelashes were. Wash it three times a day; hair will grow back quickly. This results in a full recovery, and the eyebrows and eyelashes will return to their original state, just like before.[65p]

　　浸酒法
　　苦参去上黄皮薄切曝干，捣令散，莫使作末　　右，秤取三千斤，取不津瓮受两斛者，瓮底钻作孔，着二三十青石子，如桃李鸡子许，丸过底孔上二三寸，然后下苦参、消石末、酒，一时着瓮中，遣童子年十三四者，和合调停，然后即与五六重故纸扎瓮口上，泥之莫使漏气。取酒服时，须孔中出酒服之，一日一服，或再服亦得。还如法密塞孔，勿漏泄。不得开瓮口取酒。酒欲尽时，开瓮取苦参滓，急绞取酒，其滓去却。其酒密处盛之，莫使漏气，服酒法一一如前，无有不愈。若患不瘥除者，皆由年多。[66p]

Method for Immersing Wine
Bitter sophora: remove the thick yellow skin, slice thinly, and expose to dry. Pound until it becomes coarsely powdered, avoiding a fine powder. Take three thousand jin of the sliced material, put it into a vessel that holds two dou without water. Drill holes at the bottom of the vessel and place twenty or thirty green stones, about the size of peaches, plums, or eggs, over the bottom hole by two or three inches. Then add the bitter sophora, disintegrated stone powder, and wine all at once into the vessel. Have a boy of thirteen or fourteen mix and stir well. Immediately, cover the vessel's mouth with several layers of old paper and seal it with clay to prevent air leakage. When taking the wine, ensure that it flows out through the hole; do this once a day, or even twice if necessary. Afterward, seal the hole tightly again to prevent leaking. Do not open the vessel to take the wine. When the wine nears depletion, open the vessel to retrieve the bitter sophora residue, strain to extract the wine, and discard the residue. Keep the wine in a sealed place to avoid air leakage; the method of taking the wine remains as described earlier, and there will be no failure to heal. If the ailment does not resolve after a long time, it is due to the duration of the illness.[66p]

十年者，更作此药酒至两剂，无有不愈。依法如前。虽良医治之，亦须好酒。须行忠直，不得不孝不义，患除则速矣。服药时，先令服长寿延年符，能荡除身中五脏六腑游滞，恶气皆出尽，然后服药得力，其疾速验无疑。符力亦是不可思议神力，先服药者无有不效。又生造药入瓮中时，令童子小儿和合讫，即告符书镇药。符镇在瓮腹，令药不坏，久久为好，一切神鬼不敢近之矣。　　先服此符，然后服药，一服之后，更不须再服。书符要六合日，勿令小儿女子六畜鸡犬等见之。符成不忌。　　长寿延年符[67p]

For ten years, if this medicinal wine is made into two doses, there is no ailment that cannot be cured. Follow the previous instructions. Even skilled physicians require good wine. One must act with loyalty and integrity; one must not be unfilial or unjust. When ailments are eliminated, recovery will be swift. When taking the medicine, one should first take the Longevity and Life Extension talisman, which can dispel the stagnation in the five organs and six bowels, expelling all bad energy. Then, taking the medicine will be effective, and its effects will manifest quickly and undoubtedly. The power of the talisman is also an incomprehensible spiritual force; those who take the medicine after the talisman are guaranteed to succeed.

Additionally, when creating the medicine and placing it in the jar, direct a young child to mix it well, and then announce the talisman to secure the medicine. The talisman should be placed in the belly of the jar to prevent the medicine from spoiling, ensuring its quality for a long time, keeping it safe from all spirits. First take this talisman, then take the medicine; after one dose, there is no need for further doses. The talisman should be written on a day when the heavens and the earth are in harmony, and it should not be seen by children, women, livestock, chickens, or dogs. The talisman, once completed, is unrestricted in its use.

Thunder Pill Powder
Thunder pill, red lead ground and mixed with water; one tael each of asafoetida; five taels of saltpeter; one tael finely ground, steeped in four taels of wine; finely ground realgar and orpiment, each seven and a half qian; finely ground amethyst and rhinoceros horn shavings, half a tael each; twenty each of toad and gourd seed, removing the heads, feet, and wings, stirred together with sesame until well combined, then after toasting the sesame, discard it, retaining only the toad and gourd seed. This is to be made into a fine powder. Take five taels of bitter root, crush it together with saltpeter, place in a silk cloth bag, put into a porcelain bottle, steep in one dou of clear wine for seven days, then seal tightly. Each dose is one medium cup, warmed before eating, mixed with two qian of Thunder Pill Powder.

Thunder Pill Powder
Thunder pill; finely ground realgar mixed with water; red lead mixed with water; talc; finely ground amethyst; rhinoceros horn shavings; cow bile, each half a tael; twenty each of toad and gourd seed, with heads, feet, and wings removed, also stir-fried with glutinous rice; white rattan and asafoetida, each two and a half qian. This is to be made into a fine powder, ground evenly. Each dose is one qian, mixed with empty stomach and clear wine for intake.

The two prescriptions above are based on the original formula of the master physician, supplemented and adjusted, showing effectiveness in use. Due to the difficulty in obtaining some medicines, sticking strictly to the formula might not yield completion throughout one's life. A small deviation is also acceptable; thus, they are fully detailed here.[68p]

　　白花蛇丸　丹阳荆上舍得疠疾，一僧疗之而愈，以数百金求方，秘不肯传，馆宾袁生窥知藏衲衣领中，因醉之而窃录焉，用者多效。　　白花蛇　乌梢蛇并去头尾连骨生用，各一条　漏芦半斤，洗净去苗取四两　荆芥穗一两半　防风去苗　金银花去叶　槐花　干生地黄　苦参　蝉退用草鞋踏去土　枸杞子各二两　黄芩　黄连　山栀子　黄蘗　川芎　乌药　全蝎酢浸一日去盐味　何首乌不可犯铁器　牛膝去芦　牛蒡子　连翘　细辛　白蒺藜　威灵仙　天花粉　金毛狗脊　胡麻子炒　蔓荆子各一两　　右共为细末，米糊为丸如梧桐子大，每服五六十丸，清茶送下，空心、午后、临卧各一服。一僧加风藤一两。如上头面者，加香白芷；肌肉溃烂，加大皂角各一两。[69p]

Baihua She Wan

In Danyang, at the Jing Shang She, a monk cured a man afflicted with severe illness. The man sought the formula for treatment, offering several hundred gold pieces, but the monk refused to reveal it. Yuan Sheng, a guest at the inn, learned of this by stealthily peering into the monk's collar while intoxicated and subsequently transcribed it. Many who used it found it effective.

Ingredients:

  • One each of Baihua She and Wushaoshe, with heads, tails, and bones removed
  • Half a jin of Luoluo, cleaned and purged of seedlings, to obtain four taels
  • One and a half taels of Jingjie fluff
  • Fangfeng, seedlings removed
  • Jinyin flower, leaves removed
  • Huai flower
  • Dried Shengdi Huang
  • Bitter gentian
  • Excrement of cicadas, trampled with straw sandals to remove soil
  • Two taels each of Gouqizi
  • Huangqin
  • Huanglian
  • Shanzhizi
  • Huangbo
  • Chuanxiong
  • Wuyao
  • Whole scorpion, soaked in vinegar for a day to remove the saltiness
  • He Shou Wu should not come into contact with iron utensils
  • Niu Xi, peeled
  • Niubangzi
  • Lianqiao
  • Xixin
  • Baijili
  • Weilingxian
  • Tianhuafen
  • Jinmaoguzhi
  • Fried Huama
  • One tael each of Manjingzi

Grind all the above into fine powder, mix with rice paste to create pills the size of wutong seeds. Take fifty to sixty pills each time, washed down with clear tea, once on an empty stomach, once in the afternoon, and once before sleeping. A monk adds one tael of Fengteng for treatment of wind. For those with head symptoms, add one tael of fragrant Bai Zhi; for muscle ulcers, add one tael of large soapwort.[69p]

　　大黄　白牵牛　槟榔各一两　甘草三两　轻粉五分　　右共为细末，每服二钱，用白蜜三匙，姜汁二匙调服，五更时进。病势重者，七日行一次，稍轻者半月一次，轻者一月一次或二十日一次，以三五遍为度。
　　防风天麻丸　治疠风癞病。此方料是神仙所传，一年中常疗数人。初服药有呕吐者，不可怪。服药得安如故，其效如神。　　防风去芦　天麻　升麻　白附子炮　定风草　细辛去苗　川芎　人参去芦　丹参去芦　苦参去芦　元参去芦　紫参去芦　蔓荆子　威灵仙　穿山甲炒　何首乌另捣为末，各一两　蜈蚣一对　　右为细末，与何首乌末拌匀，每药末二两，胡麻一斤，淘净晒干炒香熟，另碾为极细末，与药末一处拌匀，炼蜜和丸，共作九十丸，每服一丸细嚼，温浆水送下，不拘时候，日三服。宜食淡白粥一百二十日。病人大忌房劳，将息慎口。[70p]

Medicinal Use
Rhubarb, white gourd, and areca nut each one tael; licorice three taels; light powder five fen. Grind the above into a fine powder, take two qian each time, mixed with three spoonfuls of white honey and two spoonfuls of ginger juice, to be taken at the fifth watch (around 3-5 AM). For severe cases, administer once every seven days; for mild cases, once every half month; for light cases, once every month or every twenty days, with three to five cycles as the limit.

Preventive Wind and Celestial Hemp Pill – for treating wind phlegm and scabies. This formula is transmitted by the immortals, used to heal several people throughout the year. Initially, there may be vomiting after taking the medicine; do not be alarmed. If taking the medicine feels stable as before, its effectiveness will be miraculous. Ingredients include: Siler, Gastrodia, Cimicifuga, processed Aconite, Determined Wind Grass, Asarum (removing the sprout), Chuanxiong, Ginseng (removing the sprout), Salvia (removing the sprout), Sophora (removing the sprout), Scutellaria (removing the sprout), Purple Ginseng (removing the sprout), Vitex, Wulingxian, Stir-fried Pangolin, and He Shou Wu ground into powder, each one tael; a pair of centipedes. Grind all into a fine powder, mix with He Shou Wu powder. For every two taels of this powder, add one jin of sesame, wash clean, dry, toast until fragrant, and grind into an extremely fine powder, mix well with the medicinal powder, and refine with honey to form pills, a total of ninety pills. Take one pill, chew thoroughly, and swallow with warm water, without time constraints, three times daily. It is advisable to eat bland white porridge for one hundred twenty days. Patients should strictly avoid sexual activity, and must be cautious with their speech and rest.[70p]

　　乳香丸　治疠风神效
　　通明乳香二十两　苦参肥好者去芦銼，四两　　右先用好酒五升，浸苦参于瓶内，以重汤煮一复时，常用文武火慢熬，令小沸为候，一复时取出，滤去渣，将酒浸乳香于银砂石器内，煎如钖，入天麻四两为末，大麻仁二两另研如膏，入于乳－香膏内搅令匀，慢火熬之，可丸如梧桐子大，每服二十丸，用大麻仁酒送下，空心及晚食前服之。[71p]

He Shimo Pill - Effective in treating epidemic winds.

He Shimo is burned to retain its essence. Ingredients include pointed ends of He Shimo, licorice roasted, fragrant white atractylodes, and windbreak (each 120 grams), with 30 grams of Chuanxiong and 90 grams of five spirit resin. Clean musk and frankincense are ground separately, each 9 grams. Mix these into a fine powder, dough with wine to form pills. Make 10 pills per 60 grams. Each dose is one pill, to be chewed finely after meals, taken down with warm wine or clear tea. Two doses should be taken daily.

Lucid Frankincense Pill - Effective in treating epidemic winds.

Use 800 grams of frankincense, with 240 grams of bitter bush (remove the rough parts). First, soak the bitter bush in 5 liters of good wine within a jar, then boil with moderate heat until reduced. After cooking, filter out the residue. Soak the frankincense in this wine within a silver or stone container, simmer like incense, adding 120 grams of Tianma ground to powder. Grind 60 grams of hemp seeds into a paste and mix it with the frankincense paste for an even consistency. Simmer slowly until it thickens into pills the size of large sycamore seeds. Take 20 pills each time, with hemp seed wine, on an empty stomach or before evening meals.[71p]

Divine Immortal's Wind-Dispersing Pill
Ingredients: Motherwort, Fritillaria, Dried black plum flesh, Sea-pine bark, Golden-haired dog spine – all finely ground into equal parts. Refine with honey and form into pills, each the size of a paulownia seed. Take thirty pills daily on an empty stomach at noon and just before sleep. At night, take thirty pills urgently by your bedside before the first sleep, using the juice of sheep sorrel root to wash them down. It is strictly forbidden to consume alcohol or engage in sexual activities, as all things that provoke wind must be avoided. For one hundred days, only eat plain porridge to gradually restore skin and flesh; after six months, one must abstain from sexual activities. During the medication process, it is advised to have one or two dedicated individuals attentively watch over the patient while they sleep, to assist in taking the medicine promptly when they first wake up. The imperial envoy Huagong witnessed Lin Chengwu achieving results with this method. This treatment for epidemic wind is remarkably effective; if the prohibitions are not adhered to, it may yield no benefits.

Tianma Powder - Treats all epidemic wind and skin ailments.

Grind all ingredients finely. For each dosage, take three qian mixed with warm wine or light tea, twice daily. Take before meals for the first half month, and after meals for the next half month, yielding significant efficacy.[72p]

　　六香散　淋渫癞病，其效如神。
　　甘松去土　零陵香　香白芷　茅香去土銼　香附子炒　藿香　川芎各二两　三柰子半两　　右除三柰子另研，余七味同为(口父)咀，分作四剂，每用一剂，以水六大碗，煎至三碗，去渣，却入三柰子搅匀，乘热洗疮。若疮不破，用铍针于疙瘩疮上刺破，令恶血出尽，然后淋洗。一伏时洗一番，浴室毋令透风。卧处须令暖和得所。一月之间，不可出外，水火亦就其中，洗了拭干，用八金散点。若热不可饮冷水。[73p]

He Shou Wu Powder is used to treat skin diseases like leprosy. Take one jin of He Shou Wu, soak it in white rice water for seven days, changing the water daily in summer. Use a bamboo knife to scrape it into pieces, and then steam and sun-dry it nine times. Take four taels of sesame seeds, also steamed and sun-dried nine times. Grind them into a fine powder. Take two qian before meals, mixed with warm wine or mint soup.

Liuxiang Powder treats skin diseases effectively. Ingredients include: two taels of gan song without soil, two taels of Lingling fragrance, two taels of white aster, two taels of fragrant grass, two taels of roasted cyperus, two taels of fragrant wood, and two taels of Chuanxiong; plus half a tael of san cai zi, powdered separately. The other seven ingredients are ground together, divided into four doses. Each time, use one dose with six large bowls of water, simmer until reduced to three bowls, strain, then mix in the san cai zi. While hot, wash the sores. If the sores do not break, use a needle to prick the nodules, allowing the bad blood to drain completely, then wash again. Wash once during one treatment; ensure the bathing area is warm and not drafty. Stay indoors for a month, keeping warm and dry, wash and dry the area, and apply Ba Jin San. If feeling hot, avoid drinking cold water.[73p]

　　八金散
　　金精石　银精石　阳起石　元精石　磁石　石膏　滑石　禹余粮石。　　右件各等分碾末，入金银坩锅子内盛之，用盐泥固济口，以文武火煅炼红透，放冷，研如粉，入水银半两，轻粉一钱研，令不见星子，却入余药再研匀。令患人先洗疮拭干，便用小油调稠硬作剂子，于有疮处擦上药，兼治疙瘩。擦药之后，大忌饮水，宜禁身静坐，至三日，口中涎出为度。二次药了，用贯众汤漱口，不可咽下药汁。两手便洗净，不可近口鼻耳目。第四日一伏时，依前上药。第七日见效，不可更用。[74p]

Eight Gold Powder

Gold essence stone, silver essence stone, yangqi stone, original essence stone, magnetic stone, gypsum, talc, and Yuyuliang stone. Grind each of these items into equal parts into a fine powder, place them in a gold and silver cauldron, seal the mouth with salt mud, and refine them with delicate and strong fire until they are fully red. Allow to cool, then grind into a fine powder. Add half a tael of mercury and one qian of light powder, also ground finely so that no specks remain. Then mix with the remaining medicinal ingredients and grind evenly. The patient should first wash the sores and dry them. Prepare a thick paste with a small amount of oil and apply it to the sores, also treating any lumps. After applying the medicine, it is strictly forbidden to drink water; the patient should remain calm and seated for three days until saliva is produced. After the second treatment, rinse the mouth with Guanzhong decoction, but do not swallow the medicine. Wash the hands thoroughly and avoid contact with the mouth, nose, ears, and eyes. On the fourth day during the next application, apply the medicine as before. By the seventh day, if results are seen, no additional use is permitted.[74p]

Washing Medicine
He Shou Wu, Jing Jie, Fang Feng, Verbena, and Vitex Negundo in equal parts. Each use is ten taels, with one dou of water; decoct until boiling, wash in a windless place, resulting in sweating.

For treating eyebrow loss.

Translation:

Zi He Sheng Mei San - Treats illnesses of the wind causing the eyebrows to fall out.

Ban Xia - Divide sheep dung equally.

Grind it into a powder; apply ginger juice to the brow ridge. If there is no effect, refer to symptoms of eyebrow loss for treatment.

Wu She San - Treats ulcers of the skin caused by wind, presenting as spots like vitiligo.

Three taels of black snake, one tael of rhinoceros horn shavings, each two taels of Fang Feng, Qiang Huo, Huang Qin, and Ku Shen (with the roots removed), Ren Shen, Dan Shen, Yuan Shen, Sha Shen (with the roots removed), Gui Xin, Qin Jiao (with the roots and soil removed), Chuan Xiong, Zhi Zi Ren, Bai Xian Pi, Chuan Sheng Ma, Tong Cao, Bai Ji Li, and Zhi Ke (stir-fried away from the pulp); each one tael. Grind them into a fine powder. Take two qian with warm wine after a meal and consume. Avoid hot foods such as chicken, pork, fish, garlic, and hot noodles.

Nu Wei Gao - Treats skin ulcers with patchy spots.

Half a tael each of Nu Wei, Fu Zi, Ji She Xiang, Mu Xiang, and Bai Zhi, one qian of musk (ground separately).

Refine the above ingredients, using half a jin of pig lard in December to simmer the medicine until it turns yellow and charred, then remove the residue. Mix in the musk until uniform and let it solidify. Use coarse cloth to apply to the patchy spots; it may cause slight pain, but applying it will lead to healing.

Shu Shui Hua Gao - Treats ulcers of the skin.[76p]

　　麝香一钱，另研　蜀水花　鹰粪白　白附子　白蔹　当归各一两　　右件銼碎，用猪脂一斤，合煎诸药焦黄，去渣候冷，入麝香搅令匀，于瓷盒中盛，先擦微破涂敷之。
　　猬皮丸　治乌癞。
　　蚺蛇头烧存性　魁蛤锻粉　猬皮烧存性，各一枚　蜈蚣一条半　蝱虫去头足翅　蛴螬焙干　红娘子去头足翅　水蛭糯米炒熟　蜘蛛炒　螌蝥去头足翅，各三个　鲮鲤甲三片　龙骨研　川椒炒　川大黄　黄连　麝香研　桂心　木银各半两　石膏细研　川芒硝各一两　滑石研水飞　甘遂与胡麻同炒，以胡麻熟为度　白矾枯各二钱半　附子二枚，炮去皮脐　雷丸　巴豆去皮膜心油，各十五粒　　右为细末，入研令匀，炼蜜和丸如小豆大，每服一九，温水送下，空心临卧各一服；未觉，每服加一丸。如小便茎中痛，即有虫下，皆死也。细观形状。痛多即减一丸，痛少则加至二丸，以瘥为度。右方乃攻毒取虫之峻剂，非灼知脏腑有虫毒，及精神可胜攻下者，不可轻服。[77p]

One cash of musk, ground separately; one tael each of Shu water flower, white eagle dung, white attachia, white vine, and angelica. The above ingredients are to be finely crushed, then mixed with one pound of pig fat and fried until golden brown. Strain out the residue, let cool, add the musk and mix evenly. Store in a porcelain box and apply on slightly broken areas.

Hedgehog skin pills treat skin diseases.

The above should be ground into a fine powder, mixed evenly, and then honey is added to form pills the size of small beans. Take one every nine days, sent down with warm water, an empty stomach just before lying down. If you feel the effects, increase the dose by one pill each time. If there is pain in the urinary tract, this indicates worms passing out, all dead. Observe the shape closely. If the pain increases, reduce by one pill; if it decreases, increase up to two pills, adjusting until healed. This formula is a potent remedy for expelling toxins and worms; it should not be taken lightly unless one is certain of the presence of worms or toxins in the internal organs, and the spirit can withstand the purgation.[77p]

Based on the source of Ma Huang Xu Ming Tang
It treats lung deficiency cold, harm from fierce wind, causing wheezing and coughing, with a hoarse voice and congestion, shortness of breath and fatigue, weakness of limbs, pale complexion, loss of appetite, and cold sweats.

Directions: Grind the twelve ingredients and prepare with 1 dou 2 sheng of water. The old formula lacks bai zhu and poria, and the current formula lacks huang qin. Adjust based on the principles and adapt for the specific condition.

Baihua She San: Treats purple vitiligo.
Ingredients: 2 liang white flower snake; 2.5 qian of evening silkworm moth; stir-fried white silkworm; black rhinoceros horn powder; gastrodia; ephedra with the stems removed; tian nan sing prepared with ginger; He Shou Wu; white attached zizi (a type of herb) processed; tree bark of white xian; qing hao with the roots removed; vitex; cassia heart; qing feng with the roots removed; each half a liang; 1 liang of magnetite, vinegar-purified and ground.
Grind to a fine powder, mix well. Take 2 qian before meals, mixed with warm wine. Avoid hot noodles, pork, fish, garlic, and other such foods.[85p]

　　酸石榴丸　治紫癜风，其效如神。
　　酸石榴七枚，去皮瓷盆盛，饭甑上蒸烂，绞取汁　羌活　防风　薄荷叶　人参各一两　茺蔚子　白附子炮　苦参　乌喙　犀角屑各半两　冬消梨二十枚，去皮核捣绞取汁　　右件为末，取前二汁煎如膏，和丸如梧桐子大，每服二十丸，温酒送下，不拘时候。
　　硫黄膏　治紫癜风。
　　硫黄　白矾并细研，各一两　硇砂细研　白附子各半两　附子　雄黄细研，各七钱半　蛇蜕一条　　右为细末，入研令匀，用清油四两，黄蜡二两，先煎油三五沸，下蜡，后入药末，煎成膏，每取涂所患处，日三度用之。
　　灰藋膏　治紫癜风。
　　灰藋草不以多少，烧灰，用重纸衬水淋取汁熬膏　虾蟆灰　白矾灰　硫黄各半两　雄黄二钱　朱砂七钱半，水飞　腻粉研　麝香研，各一钱　　右各药为细末，同研令匀，用灰藋膏调涂所患处，干即再涂之。[86p]

Sour Pomegranate Pills: Treats purpura; its effect is miraculous.
Seven sour pomegranates, peeled, placed in a porcelain bowl, steamed over rice steamer until soft, and juice extracted. Add 1 tael each of Qianghuo, Fangfeng, mint leaves, and ginseng; half tael each of Chuanwuzi, Bai Fuzhu (processed), bitter sophora, Wu Hui, and rhinoceros horn powder; twenty winter pears, peeled and pitted, mashed and juice extracted. Combine the above into a powder, take the first two juices and boil down to a thick paste, then shape into pills the size of Wutong seeds. Take twenty pills with warm wine, without concern for timing.

Sulfur Ointment: Treats purpura.
Sulfur and white alum, both finely ground, 1 tael each; finely ground Niu Sha and Bai Fuzhu, half tael each; Wu Tou and finely ground Xiong Huang, 7.5 qian each; one snake skin. Combine into a fine powder and mix well. Use 4 liang of clear oil and 2 liang of yellow wax; first boil the oil to a rolling boil, add the wax, then when melted, incorporate the herbal powder, cooking until it becomes an ointment. Apply to the affected area three times a day.

Ash of Gray Fennel Ointment: Treats purpura.
The amount of gray fennel grass is not fixed; burn to ash and use heavy paper to collect the juice by soaking in water to boil into a paste. Half tael each of toad ash, white alum ash, and sulfur; 2 qian of Xiong Huang and 7.5 qian of Zhusha (cinnabar) flying in water; and 1 qian each of oily powder and powdered musk. Grind these medicinal ingredients into a fine powder and mix well. Use gray fennel ointment to apply to the affected area; apply again when dry.[86p]

　　摩风膏　治白癜风。

　　硫黄　密陀僧　腻粉　乳香并另研　杏仁　白僵蚕炒　　右为细末，酥调成膏，用浆水洗疮，以生布擦破涂之，日夜四五次，甚妙。　　又方　治白癜风。[87p]

Black Snake Powder: Treats stubborn numbness in the body and white vitiligo.
Ingredients: 3-6 ounces of black snake (soaked in wine), 2 ounces each of fried white silkworm, angelica, and sesame seeds; 2.5 taels of tian nanxing (arisaema); 1 tael each of processed fried aconite and processed white atractylodes; 1 tael each of windproof herb (processed) and xixin (asarum); 1 tael each of dried bitter orange (processed) and cinnamon heart; 0.5 tael each of cicada molting.
Grind everything into a fine powder. For each dose, take 2 taels mixed with warm wine, at any time.

Bitter Root Powder: Treats long-accumulated wind poison in the lungs and persistent white patches on the skin.
Ingredients: 3 ounces of bitter root (processed), 1 ounce each of pine resin, processed aconite, gardenia seeds, magnolia bark, and bee nest; 2 ounces of black snake (soaked in wine).
Grind everything into a fine powder. For each dose, take 2 taels mixed with warm wine, at any time.

Wind Rubbing Ointment: Treats vitiligo.
Ingredients: 2 ounces each of aconite, processed aconite, and windproof herb; 1 ounce each of thunbergia flower and bee nest.
Grind these finely, then stew with 3 pounds of lard until the medicine turns yellow and dark, then strain and let cool. Store in a porcelain box. Use to rub on vitiligo until healed.

Another Formula:
Ingredients: sulfur,密陀僧 (myrrh), oily powder, and frankincense ground separately; almonds and fried white silkworm.
Grind these into a fine powder and mix with pig fat to make an ointment. Wash the wound with watery pulp, then apply with fresh cloth, rubbing it in four to five times a day for best effect.

Another Formula: Treats vitiligo.[87p]

　　羚羊角散　治风热，皮肤生(疒咅)(疒畾)痒痛。　　羚羊角屑　乌蛇肉酒浸　川大黄　元参去芦，各一两　枳壳麸炒　白蒺藜　甘草炙，各半两　秦艽去芦土　防风去芦，各七钱半　　右件(口父)咀，每服五钱，水一中盏，煎至七分，去渣，入牛蒡根汁半合，更煎一两沸，温服，不拘时候。[88p]

Red-gray vine grass, five pounds of cocklebur root stalks, three pounds of eggplant root stalks. Dry the above items in the sun, then burn them to ash. Use one dou of water to decoct the ash, extracting the juice and then simmering it in a pan to form a paste. Store in a ceramic box, grinding half a tael of good frankincense, then adding 2.5 qian each of lead frost and greasy powder, mixing into the paste. Add two taels of rendered yellow cow fat into the paste, stirring until uniform. Apply to the affected area three times during the day and once at night.

Another prescription to treat vitiligo:
Five raw green walnuts, 2.5 qian of white alum, finely ground, half a tael of sulfur, finely ground. Mix and grind the above into a paste, applying two to three times daily until healed.

Antelope Horn Powder treats wind-heat, skin itching and pain.
Ingredients: antelope horn shavings, black snake meat soaked in wine, one tael of each; rhubarb, and radix scrophulariae (removed from pith), one tael each; half a tael each of fried bitter orange peel, white thistle, and honey-fried licorice; and 7.5 qian each of radix gentianae (removed from soil) and fangfeng (removed from pith).
Grind and take 5 qian each time, boil with one medium cup of water until reduced to seven parts, strain out the residue, add half a cup of burdock root juice, boil again until bubbling, and take warm at any time.[88p]

Qin Jiao Decoction: Treats wind heat toxin invading the skin, causing a body-wide rash like that of a hemp seed. Ingredients: Qin Jiao (prepared) 1 tael, Fang Feng (prepared), Huang Qin, Ma Huang (truncated at the nodes), Gan Cao (roasted), Yuan Shen (prepared), Rhino horn powder, Niu Bang Zi (stir-fried), Zhi Ke (dried and stir-fried) each 7.5 qian. Wu She San: Treats wind heat, causing a body-wide rash and itching. Ingredients: Wu She meat soaked in wine, 2 taels, Qiang Huo (prepared), Bai Xian Pi, Gui Xin, Gan Cao (roasted), Zhi Ke (dried and stir-fried), Pu Huang (stir-fried), Man Jing Zi, Xiong Rens, Dang Gui (prepared), each 0.5 tael, Tian Ma, Ma Huang (truncated at the nodes), Qin Jiao (prepared), Niu Bang Zi (stir-fried), Gao Ben (prepared), Bai Jiang Can (stir-fried), each 7.5 qian. Directions: Grind to a fine powder, take 2 qian each time, mix with warm wine and take at any time.

Jing Jie San: Treats wind heat, causing itching and rash on the skin. Fáng Fēng Sàn: Treats wind (syndrome).
Prepare one tael of honey-fried licorice, one tael of Fáng Fēng (remove the root), one tael of almond and wheat flour (fried separately and ground into paste), and one tael of fried silkworms. Mix these into a fine powder. Take 9 grams each time, dissolve in honey water, or warm wine, twice a day.

Zhī Lì Wán: Treats wind itch (syndrome).
Prepare one tael each of white Zhi Li, Qín Jiāo (remove the root), and red Poria (remove the skin); half a tael each of Qiāng Huó, bitter locust seed (remove the root), yellow root, and fine Xīn (remove the sprouts); and 7.5 grams of bitter orange peel (remove the fiber and fry). Use three taels of black snake meat, soaked in wine. Mix these into a fine powder, and form into pills the size of phoenix seeds. Take 30 pills at a time, with warm honey soup, at any time.

Hēi Lóng Wán: Treats wind poison attacking the head and face, often causing (syndrome).
Prepare one tael each of Qiāng Huó (remove the root), mint leaves, and Vitex, fine pine soot, and Dú Huó (remove the root); with half a tael each of Chuan Xiong, honey-fried licorice, white Aconite (stewed), mountain gardenia, Fang Feng (remove the root), Jīng Jiè flower, and Tian Nan Xing (processed with ginger juice), along with fresh black Aconite and fried silkworms, and peeled black Aconite (process the core). Mix these into a fine powder, form into pills, ten pieces for every tael. Take 19 pieces at a time, chew well, and wash down with tea or warm wine after meals.[90p]

　　莽草膏　治风瘙痒，皮肤生(疒咅)(疒畾)，体肿疼痛。　　莽草一两　当归去芦　芎藭　大戟去皮　川椒　附子　细辛去苗　赤芍药　芫花　(艹蹢)(艹躅)花　蒴藋各二两　　右细銼，用酢三升，浸一宿，用猪脂三斤同煎，令附子色黄为度，绵滤去渣，每涂摩病处，日三五上。　　又方　治风瘙痒，皮肤生(疒咅)(疒畾)，搔之成疮，宜用此粉身即瘥。　　芎藭　麻黄根銼　白芷各三两　雷丸五两　藿香二两　藜芦一两半　　右为细末，入英粉五两，相和令匀，逐日粉身上。
　　柳枝汤　治风瘙皮肤生(疒咅)(疒畾)，搔之肿痒。　　嫩柳枝　桃枝　蒴藋　苦参各五两　茵陈　狼毒　青葙叶　麻黄各三两　槐白皮四两　　右细銼和匀，每取一斤，用水五斗，煮取四斗，去渣，更入盐及(石卜)硝各二两搅匀，看冷热，于温室中洗浴，浴罢衣覆出汗瘥，切慎外风。[91p]

Mangcao Gao: Treats wind-related itching, skin lesions, swelling, and pain.

  • Ingredients:
    • 1 tael of Mangcao
    • 1 tael of Angelica, remove the coarse parts
    • 1 tael of Chuanxiong
    • 1 tael of Euphorbia, peel removed
    • 1 tael of Sichuan pepper
    • 1 tael of Aconite
    • 1 tael of Xixin, remove sprouts
    • 1 tael of Red peony
    • 1 tael of Yanhuasuo
    • 2 taels each of both Caoze and Caokuanhua

Grind finely, soak in 3 sheng of vinegar overnight, then simmer with 3 jin of pig fat until the Aconite turns yellow. Strain out the dregs and apply to the affected area 3 to 5 times daily.

Another Formula: Treats wind-related itching, skin lesions that become sores upon scratching.

  • Ingredients:
    • 3 taels of Chuanxiong
    • 3 taels of Mahuang root, crushed
    • 3 taels of Bai Zhi
    • 5 taels of Leiwan
    • 2 taels of Huoxiang
    • 1.5 taels of Lilies

Grind finely, combine with 5 taels of Yingfen, mix evenly, and apply daily.

Willow Branch Decoction: Treats wind-related itching and skin lesions that swell and itch upon scratching.

  • Ingredients:
    • 5 taels each of tender willow branches, peach branches, Caokuan, and bitter root
    • 3 taels each of Yincheng, Wolf poison, green plantain leaves, and Mahuang
    • 4 taels of white locust bark

Grind finely and mix. Take 1 jin, use 5 dou of water to boil down to 4 dou, strain out the dregs, add 2 taels each of salt and Shibukxiao. Mix thoroughly, check temperature, and use for bathing in a warm setting. After bathing, cover up and sweat to recovery; be cautious of external wind.[91p]

　　丹参汤　治风热，皮肤生(疒咅)(疒畾)，苦痒成疥。　　丹参　苦参各四两　蛇床子生用，三两　　右件药，用水一斗五升，煎至七升，去渣，乘热洗之。
　　垂柳汤　治皮肤风热，生疮(疒咅)(疒畾)，或痒痛。　　杨柳一斤　杏仁　白矾生用，各三两　　右件用水一斗五升，煎至七升，去渣，于无风处洗浴极妙。
　　　　单方

　　大风疠疾，眉发堕落，遍身顽痹：禹余粮二斤，白矾、青盐各一斤为末，罐子固济，炭火一秤煅之，从辰至戌，候冷研粉，埋土中三日取出，每一两，和入九蒸九暴炒熟胡麻末三两，每服二钱，荆芥汤下。【《圣惠》】
　　大风及丹石热风，手足不遂：用消石一两，生乌麻油二斤，置铛中，以土墼盖口，纸泥固济火煎，初时气腥，热则气－香；更以生麻油二斤，合煎得所，收不津器中。服时坐室中，作小低屋燃火于内，服一大合发汗，力壮者日二服，三七日头面疱疮皆灭也。必以燃火为使。【婆　门僧方】[92p]

Dan Shen Decoction: Treats wind-heat, skin lesions (itching and pain), resulting in scabs. Ingredients: 4 ounces of Danshen, 4 ounces of Ku Shen, 3 ounces of She Chuang Zi (used raw). Combine with 1.5 dou of water, boil down to 7 sheng, strain out the dregs, and wash while hot.

Willow Decoction: Treats skin wind-heat, sores (itching and pain). Ingredients: 1 jin of willow, 3 ounces each of raw apricot kernels and white alum. Boil in 1.5 dou of water down to 7 sheng, strain out the dregs, and wash in a wind-free area; it is exceedingly effective.

Single Recipe

For severe wind diseases, hair loss, and widespread stubborn paralysis: use 2 jin of Yu Yu Liang, and grind 1 jin each of white alum and green salt into a fine powder, compressing in a jar. Heat with charcoal for 3 hours, then let cool and grind the powder; bury underground for 3 days. For each dose, mix 1 tael with 3 ounces of roasted sesame powder (cooked using the nine steaming and nine drying method). Take 2 qian with Jing Jie Decoction.

For severe wind and heat from Dan Shi, with paralysis of the limbs: use 1 tael of Xiao Shi and 2 jin of raw black sesame oil. Place in a pot sealed with earth and paper clay, simmer until the initial smell changes from fishy to fragrant. Then add another 2 jin of raw sesame oil and continue to cook to the desired point, storing in a non-hydrating container. When taking, sit in a low-roofed room with a fire inside, consuming a large dose to induce sweating. For strong individuals, take twice daily for 37 days until facial sores disappear. It is crucial to use the fire as directed.[92p]

　　疠风有虫：硫黄末酒调少许饮汁，或加大风子油更好。【《直指方》】
　　大风癞疮，乃营气不清，久风入脉，因而成癞，鼻坏色败：用黄精根去皮净，以水洗二斤，暴纳粟米饭中，蒸至米熟时食之。【《总录》】　　又方：用苦参五两切，以好酒三斗，渍三十日，每饮一合，日三服，常服不绝，若觉痹即瘥。【苏颂】　　又方：用苦参末二两，以猪肚盛之，缝合煮熟，取出去药，先饿一日，次早先饮新水一盏，将猪肚食之，如吐再食；待一二时，以肉汤调服无忧散五七钱，取出大小虫一二万为效。后以不蛀皂角一斤，去皮子煮汁，入苦参调糊，下何首乌末二两，防风末一两半，当归末一两半，芍药末五钱，人参末三钱，丸梧子大，每服三五十九，温酒或茶下，日三服；仍用麻黄、苦参、荆芥煎水洗之。[93p]

For pestilential winds with insects: Mix a small amount of powdered sulfur with wine and drink it, or adding more oil from the large wind seeds is better. [From "Direct Treatment Recipes"]

For large wind leprosy, it is caused by unclear vital energy and prolonged exposure to wind entering the channels, resulting in leprosy, with the nose rotting and color deteriorating: Use two pounds of fresh peeled rhizome of Huang Jing, wash it with water, then mix it with millet rice, and steam until the rice is cooked and eat it. [From "Comprehensive Record"]

Another recipe: Take five ounces of bitter root, chop it, and soak it in three dou of fine wine for thirty days. Drink one measure three times a day, and continue without interruption; if you feel numbness, it will be cured. [Su Song]

Another recipe: Take two ounces of powdered bitter root, place it in a pig's stomach, sew it up, and boil it. Remove the medicine, fast for one day, then drink a cup of fresh water in the morning, then eat the pig's stomach. If there is vomiting, eat again; wait for one to two hours, and mix five to seven qian of Wuyou powder in meat broth and take it to expel thousands of small insects. Afterwards, take one pound of uninfested soap pod, remove the skin, boil it for juice, mix it with bitter root to form a paste, add two ounces of He Shou Wu powder, one and a half ounces of Fang Feng powder, one and a half ounces of Dang Gui powder, five qian of Shao Yao powder, and three qian of Ren Shen powder, making pills the size of a wutou. Take three to five every day with warm wine or tea, three times a day; further, wash with the decoction of Ma Huang, bitter root, and Jing Jie.[93p]

　　恶疮癞疾：但是恶疮遍体，面目有疮者，皆可服之。用白艾蒿十束如升大者，取汁，以曲及米一如酿酒法候熟，稍稍服之。【《梅师方》】
　　白癞风疮：干艾随多少，以浸曲酿酒如常法，日饮之，觉痹即瘥。【《肘后方》】
　　大风疠疾：用嫩苍耳、荷叶等分为末，每服二钱，温酒下，日二服。【《袖珍方》】　　又方：用苍耳叶为末，以大枫子油和丸梧子大，每服三四十丸，以茶汤下，日二服。【《乾坤生意》】　　又方：五月五日或六月六日，五更带露采苍耳草，捣取汁，熬作锭子；取半斤鲤鱼一尾，剖开不去肚肠，入药一锭，线缝，以酒二碗，慢火煮熟令吃，不过三五个鱼即愈也。忌盐一百日。
　　大风癞疮：大黄煨、皂角刺各一两为末，每服方寸匕，空心温酒下，取出恶毒物如鱼脑状，未下再服，即取下如乱发之虫。取尽乃服雄黄花蛇药，名通天再造散。【《十便良方》】[94p]

Erysipelas and Leprosy: For those who are afflicted with widespread sores or facial lesions, they may take this remedy. Use ten bundles of white mugwort, crush them to extract the juice, and mix it with fermented rice as if brewing wine, then take it gradually.

Leprosy and Skin Sores: Use dry mugwort in appropriate amounts, soak it to brew wine as per the usual method, consume daily, and once the symptoms of numbness appear, it will heal.

Severe Wind Disease: Grind equal parts of tender ragweed and lotus leaves, taking 6 grams with warm wine, twice daily. Another method involves grinding ragweed leaves and mixing them with oil from the big maple seed to form pills the size of a walnut, taking 30 to 40 pills with tea soup, twice daily. Additionally, on the fifth day of the fifth month or the sixth day of the sixth month, gather ragweed in the early morning dew, pound to extract the juice, and cook it into a pill. Take half a pound of carp, cut it open without removing the entrails, insert one pill of medicine, sew it closed, and slowly cook in two bowls of wine until ready to eat; it should take no more than three to five fish for recovery. Avoid salt for a hundred days.

Severe Wind Leprosy: Take 30 grams each of roasted rhubarb and soapwort thorn, grind them to a powder, and take a pinch on an empty stomach with warm wine, until harmful substances like fish brain are expelled. If not discharged, continue taking until removed like tangled hair worms. After all are expelled, take the medicinal powder called "Tongtian Rebirth Powder."[94p]

　　疠风鼻塌，手足挛曲，节间痛不可忍，渐至断落：用蓖麻子一两去皮，黄连一两銼豆大，以小瓶子入水一升同浸，春夏二日，秋冬五日，后取蓖麻子一枚劈破，面东以浸药水吞之，渐加至四五枚，微利不妨。瓶中水尽更添。两月后吃大蒜猪肉试之，如不发是效也。如发动再服，直候不发乃止。【《杜壬方》】
　　大风恶癞：三月四月采天雄乌头苗及根，去土勿洗，捣汁渍细粒黑豆摩去皮不落者，一夜取出，晒干又浸，如此七次。初吞三枚，渐加至六七枚。禁房室猪肉鸡蒜，犯之即死。
　　大风癣疮，遍身黑色，肌体麻木，痹痛不常：草乌头一斤刮洗去皮，极净摊干，以清油四两、盐四两，同入铫内，炒令深黄色，倾出剩油，只留盐并药再炒，令黑烟出为度。取一枚劈破，心内如米一点白者始好，白多者再炒，乘热，杵罗为末，酢面和丸梧子大，每服三十丸，空心温酒下。草乌性毒难制，五七日间，以黑豆煮粥食解其毒。【《澹寮方》】[95p]

The text discusses various remedies for specific ailments. Here’s the translation:

For the disease characterized by a collapsed nose and distorted hands and feet, with unbearable pain in the joints leading to eventual loss of limbs: use one ounce of peeled castor beans and one ounce of yellow gentian, size of large beans, soak these in one liter of water in a small bottle. Soak for two days in spring and summer, and five days in autumn and winter. Afterward, take one castor bean, break it, face east, and swallow it immersed in the medicinal water. Gradually increase to four or five beans; a slight benefit is not a problem. Add more water to the bottle as it diminishes. After two months, try eating garlic and pork; if it does not react, the remedy is effective. If an issue arises, continue taking until there is no reaction.

For the severe wind-leprosy: in March and April, harvest the seedlings and roots of Aconitum and do not wash off the soil. Grind the juice to soak small black beans, rubbing off the skins that do not fall off. After one night, take them out, dry them, and soak them again, repeating this seven times. Initially swallow three beans, gradually increase to six or seven beans. Avoid pork, chicken, and garlic in the living quarters; violating this may lead to death.

For the wind-scald disease, with widespread black spots on the body, accompanied by numbness and intermittent pains: take one pound of black Aconitum, scrape and wash off the skins thoroughly, then dry it. Mix with four ounces of clear oil and four ounces of salt in a pan, stir-fry until a deep yellow color. Pour out the excess oil, leaving only the salt and medicine, and stir-fry until black smoke is released. Take one piece, break it, and if there is a small white point like rice in the center, it is good; if more white, continue frying. While hot, grind to a powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of walnuts, taking thirty pills each time with warm wine on an empty stomach. The black Aconitum is very toxic; it is advisable to consume porridge made with black beans over five or seven days to counteract the poison.[95p]

　　疠风有虫，眉落声变：预知子膏。用预知子、雄黄各二两为末，以乳香三两，同水一斗，银锅煮至五升，入二末熬成膏，瓶盛之，每服一匙，温酒调下，有虫如尾，随大便而出。【《圣惠方》】
　　大风疠疾：凌霄花五钱，地龙焙、僵蚕炒、全蝎炒各七个为末，每服二钱，温酒下。先以药汤浴过。服此出臭汗为效。《事亲》加蝉蜕、五品各九个，作一服。【《家珍》】
　　遍体癞疮：葎草一担，以水二石，煮取一石渍之，不过三作愈。【《独行方》】
　　乌癞风疮：葎草三秤切洗，益母草一秤切，以水二石五斗，煮取一石五斗，去渣，入瓮中浸浴一时，方出坐密室中，入暖汤浴一时乃出，暖卧取汗，勿令见风。明日又浴。如浴时瘙痒不可忍，切勿搔动，少顷渐定。　　后隔三日一作，以愈为度。【《总录》】[96p]

Diseases caused by pestilence: When afflicted by pestilential winds, there are worms, resulting in changes to the voice. For remedy, take two taels each of Yu Zhi Zi and Xiong Huang, powdered; combine with three taels of milk incense and a measure of water (one dou), boil in a silver pot until reduced to five sheng. Add the powders, simmer until a thick paste forms, and store in a bottle. Take one spoonful mixed with warm wine to expel worms resembling tails, which will emerge with stool.

For major wind and pestilence: take five qian of Lingxiao flower, seven each of earth dragon (baked), silkworm (stir-fried), and scorpion (stir-fried), ground into powder. Take two qian with warm wine; first bathe using a decoction of the herbs. Sweating profusely is the intended effect. From the "Shiqin" prescription, add nine of each of the cicada exuviae and the five brands as one dosage.

For extensive scabs all over the body: Take one dan of Liu grass, boil with two石 of water, to obtain one 石 of concentrated liquid; this should be done no more than three times for healing.

For dark scabby sores: Take three qing of Liu grass, cut and wash, and one qing of Yi Mu Cao, cut as well. Use two石 and five dou of water to boil down to one 石 and five dou. Remove the residue, place in a vessel for soaking for a period, then emerge to soak in warm water for a time; keep warm to induce sweating, avoiding exposure to wind. Bathe again the following day. If itching becomes intolerable during bathing, do not scratch; it will gradually subside after a moment. After three days, repeat as needed until healed.[96p]

　　大风癞疾：百灵藤四两，水一斗，煮三升，去渣，入粳米四合煮粥，于密室中浴毕乃食，暖卧取汗，汗后皮肤起如麸片。每隔日一作，五六十日后渐愈，毛发即生。【《圣惠》】　　又方：浮萍草三月采，淘三五次，窨三五日，焙为末，不得见日，每服三钱，食前温酒下。常持观音圣号。忌猪鱼面蒜。　　又方：七月七日，取紫背浮萍日干为末半升，入好消风散五两，每服五钱，水煎频饮，仍以煎汤洗浴之。【《十便良方》】
　　大风疮裂：大枫子烧存性，和麻油、轻粉研涂，仍以壳煎汤洗之。【《卫生方》】
　　恶疾风疮：狼毒、秦艽等分为末，每服方寸匕，温酒下，日一二服。【《千金》】
　　大风疠疾：大麻仁三升淘晒，以酒一斗，浸一夜，研取白汁，滤入瓶中，重汤煮数沸收之，每饮一小盏，兼服茄根散、乳香丸取效。【《圣惠》，下同。】[97p]

Severe Wind-related Illness:

For severe wind ailments, take four taels of Larkspur vine and one dou of water, boil it down to three sheng, strain out the dregs, and add four he of glutinous rice to cook porridge. After bathing in a secluded room, consume the porridge, lie down warmly to induce sweating. After sweating, the skin will rise like bran flakes. Repeat every other day, and gradually, after fifty to sixty days, recovery will occur, with regrowth of hair.

Another Recipe:

Collect floating pondweed in the third month, rinse three to five times, soak for three to five days, and grind to a powder without exposing it to sunlight. Take three qian with warm wine before meals. Constantly recite the name of Avalokiteshvara. Avoid pork, fish, and garlic.

Yet Another Recipe:

On the seventh day of the seventh month, take half a sheng of sun-dried purple-backed floating pondweed, mix it with five liang of medicinal wind-dispelling powder, and take five qian each time, boiled with water to drink frequently. Use the decoction for bathing as well.

Severe Wind Ulcers:

Burn large maple seeds to a charcoal state, mix with sesame oil and lycopodium powder for application, and wash with the shell decoction.

Nasty Wind Ulcers:

Grind equal parts of wolf poison and gentian into a powder, taking a small spoonful with warm wine once or twice daily.

Severe Wind Epidemic Illness:

Wash three sheng of hemp seeds, soaking them in one dou of wine overnight. Grind to extract the white juice, filter into a bottle, and boil the liquid until reduced. Drink a small cup, while also taking eggplant root powder and myrrh pills for effect.[97p]

　　大风恶疮：松叶、猪肉二斤，麻黄去节五两銼，以生绢袋盛，清酒一斗浸之，春夏五日，秋冬七日，每温服一小盏，常令醺醺，以效为度。
　　大风疠疾：摩勒香一斤，即乳头内光明者，细研，入牛乳五升，甘草末四两，磁盒盛之，安桌子上，置中庭，安剑一口，夜于北极下梼祝，去盒子盖，露一夜；次日入甑中，蒸熟三斗米熟即止。夜间依前祝露，又蒸，如此三次乃止。每服一茶匙，空心及晚食前温酒调服，服后当有恶物出，至三日三夜乃愈也。　　又方：用黄蘗末、皂角刺灰各三钱，研匀，空心酒服，取下虫物，并不损人。食白粥两三日，服补气药数剂。名神效散。如四肢肿，用针刺出水再服。忌一切鱼肉发风之物。[98p]

For severe wind disease, where the hair and eyebrows do not grow: grind the leaves of the arborvitae, steamed and sun-dried nine times, into powder; form into pills the size of paulownia seeds. Take five to ten pills each time, three times a day and once at night. After taking for a hundred days, one will recover.

For severe wind sores: take two pounds of pine needles and five ounces of chopped pig meat, place in a burlap bag. Soak in one dou of clear wine for five days in spring and summer, and seven days in autumn and winter. Warm it and take one small cup regularly, keeping oneself slightly tipsy to gauge the effectiveness.

For severe wind disease: take one pound of myrrh, specifically the luminous inner milk; finely grind it and mix with five liters of cow’s milk and four ounces of licorice powder. Store in a ceramic box placed on a table in the courtyard, with a sword positioned above, pray to the North Star overnight, then uncover the box to expose it for one night. The next day, steam it together with three douch of rice until cooking is complete. Repeat this overnight exposure and steaming two more times. Each time, take a teaspoonful, mixing with warm wine before meals and before sleeping; after taking, one should expect to expel toxins, fully recovering within three days and nights.

Another prescription: take three qian each of yellow sputum powder and soapberry thorn ash, grind them together, and take on an empty stomach with alcohol to expel parasites without harming the person. Eat plain porridge for two to three days and take several doses of qi-enhancing medicine. This is called the Divine Efficacy Powder. If limbs are swollen, prick with a needle to let out water and continue taking. Avoid all fish and meat that induce wind conditions.[98p]

取下虫大小长短，其色不一，约一二升，其病乃愈也。【《仁存方》】　　又方：杨花四两，捣成饼贴壁上，待干取下，米泔水浸一时取起，瓦焙研末二两；白花蛇、乌蛇各一条，去头尾酒浸取肉；全蝎、蜈蚣、蟾酥、雄黄各五钱，苦参、天麻各一两为末，水煎麻黄豉汁熬膏，和丸梧子大，朱砂为衣，每服五十丸，温酒下，一日三服，以愈为度。【《集效良方》】　　又方：大枫子油一两，苦参末三两，入少酒，糊丸梧子大，每服五十丸，空心温酒下，仍以苦参汤洗之。【《普济方》】[99p]

Strong winds and severe ailments cause hair and eyebrows to fall out: Use hot soup made with mulberry branches and ash to wash the head and face. Use a paste made from soybeans and water to improve the taste of the ash. Then use cooked water to wash with mung bean flour; wash the head every three days and the face daily, and recovery will be complete in no more than ten washes.

For severe wind and scaly skin: Use a solution of horseshoe crab bile. Take half a tael each of horseshoe crab bile, raw white alum, green alum, fatty powder, mercury, and musk, grinding until the stars are not visible. Take one qian with well water, using five-colored saliva for the best effect.

For sores and scabs: Take one tael of dried toads roasted, and roast a strip of soap until cooked, skin it and dip in alcohol and roast again to make a powder. Use a bamboo tube to insert it into sheep intestines and secure, place it in a steamer with bran above, steam it until cooked, then add half a qian of musk, mash with the bran and form into pills the size of a nut; take twenty-one pills warm with wine.

For itching from pestilential winds: Use earth-free white-necked earthworms, grind with jujube flesh into pills the size of a nut, and take sixty pills with fine wine. Avoid ginger and garlic.[100p]

　　疠风成癞：祛风散。用东行蝎虎一条焙干，大蚕沙五升，水淘炒，各为末，以小麦面四升，拌作络索，晒干研末，每服一二合，煎柏叶汤下，日三服，取效。【《宝鉴》】
　　大风龙胆膏：治大风疾神效。用冬瓜一个，截去五寸长，去瓤，掘地坑深三尺，令净，安瓜于内，以乌蛇胆一个，消梨一个，置于瓜上，以土隔盖之。至三七日看一度，瓜未甚坏；候七七日，三物俱化为水，在瓜皮内取出，每用一茶匙，以酒和服之，三两次立愈。小可风疾，每服一匙头。【《博济方》】
　　治癞：白花蛇膏。白花蛇五寸，酒浸去皮骨炙干，雄黄一两，水飞研匀，以白沙蜜一斤，杏仁一斤，去皮研烂，同炼为膏，每服一钱，温酒化下，日三。须先服通天再造散，下去虫物，乃服此除根。【《三因》】　　又方：白花蛇、乌梢蛇各取净肉二钱，酒炙雄黄二钱，大黄五钱为末，每服二钱，白汤下，三日一服，名白花蛇散。【洁古】[101p]

Lè Fēng Chéng Lài: To dispel wind and reduce ailments: Use one dried scorpion; five sheng of silkworm sand, washed and fried, ground into powder; mix with four sheng of wheat flour, form into strings, dry and grind into powder. Take one to two qian with a decoction of cedar leaves, three times daily for effect. [“Bǎo Jiàn”]

Dà Fēng Lóng Dǎn Gāo: For the treatment of severe wind conditions with miraculous effects: Use one winter melon, cut off five inches, remove the pulp, dig a pit three feet deep, clean it, place the melon inside, add one black snake gall and one pear, covering with earth. Check after thirty-seven days; if the melon is not badly spoiled, wait another forty-nine days. The three items will turn to liquid inside the melon skin. Take one teaspoon mixed with alcohol, three or two times will lead to immediate recovery. For minor wind conditions, take one teaspoon at a time. [“Bó Jì Fāng”]

Zhi Lài: Treat with white flower snake gall: Five inches of white flower snake, soaked in wine, peel the bones, and dry it; one liang of realgar, powdered with water and mixed well; one jin of white sugar honey and one jin of peeled almonds ground to a paste, combine to make a gall. Take one qian mixed with warm wine, three times daily. First, take Tongtian Zaizao powder to expel parasites, then take this to eliminate the root. [“Sān Yīn”] Another prescription: Use two qian of clean meat from white flower snake and black-striped snake, realgar roasted in wine (two qian), and five qian of rhubarb, ground into powder. Take two qian with white soup, every three days, known as White Flower Snake Powder. [“Jié Gǔ”][101p]

　　疠风手足麻木，眉毛脱落，皮肤瘙痒，及一切风疮：白花蛇、乌梢蛇、土蝮蛇各一条，并酒浸取肉晒干，苦参头末四两为末，以皂角一斤切，酒浸，去酒，以水一碗，挼取浓汁，石器熬膏，和丸梧子大，每服七十丸，煎通圣散下，以粥饭压之，日三服。三日一浴，取汗避风。名三蛇愈风丹。《治例》无蝮蛇，有大枫子肉三两。
　　大风：用乌蛇三条，蒸熟取肉焙，研末，蒸饼丸米粒大，以喂乌鸡，待尽，杀鸡烹熟，取肉焙研末，酒服一钱，或蒸饼丸服，不过三五鸡即愈。【《朝野佥载》】　　又方：大乌蛇一条，打死盛之待烂，以水二碗浸七日，去皮骨，入糙米二升，浸一日晒干；用白鸡一只，饿一日，以米饲之，待毛羽脱去，杀鸡煮熟食，以酒下之，吃尽。以热汤一盆，浸洗大半日，其病自愈。【《秘韫》】
　　白癞：大蝮蛇一条，勿令伤，以酒一斗渍之，糠火温令稍热，取蛇一寸，和腊月猪脂捣敷。【《肘后方》】[102p]

To treat symptoms such as numbness in hands and feet caused by pestilential wind, hair loss, skin itching, and all kinds of wind sores: take one each of a white flower snake, a black-scaled snake, and a Chinese viper; soak the meat in wine and dry it in the sun. Grind four taels of the bitter bolboschoenus roots into a powder, chop one jin of soap pods, soak in wine, then remove the wine and extract the thick juice with one bowl of water. Boil this in a stone vessel to make a paste, forming pills the size of a Wutong nut. Take seventy pills with a decoction of Tongsheng powder, pressing them down with congee or rice, three times daily. Bathe every three days to sweat and avoid the wind. This is called the "Three Snake Wind-Curing Pill." According to the "Regulations on Treatment," if viper is not available, use three taels of large sorghum fruit flesh instead.

For a severe wind condition: use three black snakes, steam to cook and remove the meat, grind it into powder, and form pills the size of rice grains to feed to a black chicken. Once consumed, slaughter the chicken, cook it, and dry the meat into powder. Take one qian with wine, or take the steamed rice pills, and within three to five chickens, one will recover.

Another method: take one large black snake, beat it to death and let it rot, then soak it in two bowls of water for seven days. Remove the skin and bones, and soak two sheng of brown rice for one day and dry it. Use one white chicken, fast it for one day, then feed it rice until its feathers fall out. Slaughter the chicken, cook it, and consume with wine. Once eaten, soak it in a hot soup for half a day, and the illness will heal itself.

For white leprosy: take one large viper, ensuring it is unharmed, and soak it in one dou of wine. Heat bran over a fire until warm, take one inch of the snake and mix it with the fat of a pig killed in the twelfth lunar month to apply.[102p]
